<span id="freeTextContainer14082827586714349535">I have a new favorite author: Jo Nesbo. (No doubt kudos are owed to the unsung translator, too.) The Son is one of the best police procedural/action/crime novels I've read in the last 12 months. The characters, even minor ones, ring true, with the single exception (to me) of Kari Adel, who seemed to exist solely as a conduit for communicating facts to the reader which wouldn't have been in the possession of one of the other main characters - but this is a minor criticism. Plot pacing, complexity</span>
  <span id="freeText14082827586714349535" style="display:none">I have a new favorite author: Jo Nesbo. (No doubt kudos are owed to the unsung translator, too.) The Son is one of the best police procedural/action/crime novels I've read in the last 12 months. The characters, even minor ones, ring true, with the single exception (to me) of Kari Adel, who seemed to exist solely as a conduit for communicating facts to the reader which wouldn't have been in the possession of one of the other main characters - but this is a minor criticism. Plot pacing, complexity, authenticity, consistency - The Son has it all - even a generally "happy" ending - in the context of this genre. I'd swear Nesbo is a Poe fan for his approach to writing - nary a wasted or superfluous word, and each one is well-chosen. <br /><br />I look forward to spending the rest of the summer reading Nesbo's previously published works!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14082827586714349535" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText6130693318012116387" style="display:none">After reading and thoroughly enjoying Nesbo‚Äôs Headhunters, I dived into this one: my second Nesbo book. <div id="review_997349324" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/997349324" />
    <a title="Doreen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8083149-doreen"><img alt="Doreen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523895144p2/8083149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/997349324?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Doreen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Doreen" href="/user/show/8083149-doreen">Doreen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8083149-doreen?shelf=personal-library">personal-library</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer997349324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10509784361282896962">I am a great admirer of Jo Nesbo‚Äôs books. I‚Äôve read all ten books in the Harry Hole series as well as <i>Headhunters</i>. Unfortunately, this standalone just doesn‚Äôt reach the level I‚Äôve come to expect of Nesb√∏. <br/><br/>Thirty-year-old Sonny Lofthus has been in prison for a dozen years. His life took a tailspin when his father, a police officer, committed suicide just as he was about to be exposed as an informant to a criminal mastermind. In return for a steady supply of heroin, Sonny has served as a scapegoat</span>
  <span id="freeText10509784361282896962" style="display:none">I am a great admirer of Jo Nesbo‚Äôs books. I‚Äôve read all ten books in the Harry Hole series as well as <i>Headhunters</i>. Unfortunately, this standalone just doesn‚Äôt reach the level I‚Äôve come to expect of Nesb√∏. <br /><br />Thirty-year-old Sonny Lofthus has been in prison for a dozen years. His life took a tailspin when his father, a police officer, committed suicide just as he was about to be exposed as an informant to a criminal mastermind. In return for a steady supply of heroin, Sonny has served as a scapegoat, confessing to crimes he didn‚Äôt commit. Then Sonny learns that his father was not a corrupt cop and had in fact been murdered. He escapes and sets out to put things right.<br /><br />From the title onwards, the book is full of religious symbolism. Sonny is an in-house saviour; fellow inmates see him as ‚Äúsome kind of saint‚Äù (343) with ‚Äúhealing hands‚Äù (3). One man experiencing Sonny‚Äôs touch describes its miraculous effect: ‚ÄúAnd it was as if heat exuded from it and spread to his chest, stomach, arms and legs‚Äù (315). He listens to confessions and dispenses absolution and blessings: ‚Äú‚ÄôAll earthly and heavenly gods have mercy on you and forgive your sins. You will die, but the soul of the penitent sinner shall be lead to Paradise. Amen. . . . Salaam alaikum‚Äô‚Äù (6 ‚Äì 7). He impresses everyone with his courtesy, comes to the aid of a boy who is bullied, and gives money to the homeless. He has an ‚Äúappealing face‚Äù (mentioned three times on page 106), and his smile ‚Äúsoftened stiff muscles and soothed hurt feelings‚Äù (107). He has a charisma and gentle demeanour that draw people to him. He is called ‚ÄúBuddha with the Sword‚Äù and ‚ÄúThe Angel from Hell‚Äù and is described as having a crucifix on his forehead (374). At one point Sonny is wounded by a bullet in his side and one of the bad guys ‚Äúprobed the bandage around his waist . . . He dug his fingers in, squeezed the flesh and pulled it out‚Äù (374) in imitation of doubting St. Thomas. The novel‚Äôs climax even occurs in a church! And the police commissioner is named Pontius!<br /><br />Sonny‚Äôs actions require too much suspension of disbelief. He is able to quit a twelve-year heroin habit cold turkey and escapes a maximum-security prison. And then there‚Äôs the break-<b>in</b>! Despite the fact that he has been in prison since the age of 18 and doesn‚Äôt know how to use a cell phone, he has amazing street smarts and manages to outwit criminal masterminds. He has one driving lesson but manages to drive himself away from a shoot-out. <br /><br />It is not only Sonny who is unbelievable. The behaviour of others is equally unrealistic. The Twin, the criminal overlord, has preternatural knowledge of goings on in Oslo. As does Sonny. (How does he know Markus‚Äôs name?) And the love story just doesn‚Äôt make any sense given the woman‚Äôs life experience. <br /><br />The main police investigator, Simon Kefas, Nesb√∏ has taken pains to portray as a convincing round character with strengths and weaknesses. With other characters, he has been less successful. There are some stock characters like the arrogant but incompetent investigator from the Norwegian National Criminal Investigation Service, and the corrupt prison warden. The villains are truly villainous with no redeeming qualities. <br /><br />All of this is not to say that the book itself does not have any redeeming qualities. It is fast-paced and suspenseful with a lot of twists and turns, though the identity of the mole is no great surprise. Some scenes struck me as being perfect for an action-packed film adaptation. Unfortunately, despite its many religious connotations, the book was not divinely inspired. <br /><br /><b>Please check out my reader's blog (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://schatjesshelves.blogspot.ca/">http://schatjesshelves.blogspot.ca/</a>) and follow me on Twitter (@DCYakabuski).</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10509784361282896962" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d6klWpAXUvvRqJj7xERjaiUS/htncjx2VGe6S4MJEFbIaWlOMv67F5TNOVZGZ8ZU9AP9gBKSYzanOe+AaPNTUQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8sgSZrqPwjGVjtGXTsAGb1bH+gbObrHGYpziv8YVA69NCF5yGGYr3dDrcDrM46NRh9b5nbuO7oaRwrd0Le9AqA==')})
  }

Nesb√∏ graduated from the Norwegian School of Economics with a degree in economics.   <span id="freeText443644505455247225" style="display:none">Jo Nesb√∏ is a bestselling Norwegian author and musician. He was born in Oslo and grew up in Molde. Nesb√∏ graduated from the Norwegian School of Economics with a degree in economics. Nesb√∏ is primarily famous for his crime novels about Detective Harry Hole, but he is also the main vocals and songwriter for the Norwegian rock band Di Derre.
